Short review: Great service! Very highly recommend!

Long review: I needed service to my late-90s 4Runner without warning - suddenly throwing codes and driving terribly. Looked up nearby shops and after seeing several positive reviews dropped off my car with the IAC team.
By the next morning (due to my no-notice drop off when they were busy) I had a full email and breakdown of the solution/fix to the problem I came in with, along with a list of all age/mileage related issues with my car. As well as a phone call to discuss that email and those issues. Some of them I was aware of, others I was not. But, after 20+ years even a low-mileage-for-the-age car needs work.
After some short research through my own records of past services to double check a few unknown variables, I went by IAC and talked with David in person a bit more about my options.
I decided to move forward with some major services that I already knew were needed, and others I was unaware of but were just as important to do immediately.
The team there had my car finished several days ahead of time to get it back before the weekend.
David was incredibly friendly, and transparent with all needs of my vehicle, and prompt in all interactions regarding service and updates.
Pricing was very fair and at no point did I feel I was being taken advantage of in the least - and I say this as someone who has worked in/around the auto industry and has personal friends who are auto shop owners.

No one likes dealing with car issues and researching shops, and while I'm very familiar with vehicles, lifespan of parts, approx service timeframes, etc.. And while a direct discussion with David giving me straight "Look, here's what we found.." isn't going to scare me, I know it would terrify others.
So for that reason, the transparency of the services/work I had done, promptness of all updates/questions/needs, and both the compassion and personableness of the staff, I couldn't recommend these guys more.
So for those reading all these reviews wondering "Can I trust this shop?". Yes. You definitely can.</Text>

< Text>
I got a puppy last year(Riley) and I started going here because it was the closest vet to my new house. Very friendly staff and clean office. The puppy package was well worth it, which included visits, shots, heartworm tests, etc. for the full first year of my puppy's life. Truly outstanding care and affordable!!

Speaking of OUTSTANDING care, Dr. Kwon is so thorough!! Before my dog got fixed, Dr. Kwon made sure that my husband and I had a clear understanding of the procedure.

For example, he personally called us before the surgery to let us know exactly when he would be starting, and gave us an update on Riley's well-being up to that point. He also called us immediately after the surgery to let us know that they were all finished and gave us another update on Riley's well-being post surgery. He made sure we had follow-up appointments set, so that he could monitor the healing process. When I picked Riley up, the doctor used a visual aid to further explain what exactly was done during surgery. He even waited after business hours, so that I could still pick up Riley after I got off work. Thank you Dr. Kwon and staff!!

If you are looking for a vet, this is certainly the place to go!! Dr. Kwon knows Riley's name when we come into the office, and he refers to Riley as "your baby" when we talk. This office gets it!! Great job!!<//Text>

< Text>
Dr. Kwon and his team are amazing. Petey (adult rescue schnauzer mix) and I have been regular visitors for the past two years. As this is a newly built facility, it has a very jazzed up modern feel. However, beyond the optics, special praise goes to the care and attitude demonstrated by Dr. Kwon and his staff. He sits down with you and explains carefully any issues, the effects of the illness/treatment and following steps. I have never left feeling confused or unsure about anything and they have been very responsive in answering follow up questions or in case of emergencies.

Dr. Kwon and the team have gone the extra mile to to work with my schedule and were often very generous with the services they provided. Through my employer, I had pet insurance. However, when I had difficulties with them (often!), Dr. Kwon stepped up with providing copies of invoices multiple times, getting on the phone with the insurance company and making recommendations on other insurance providers.

Alas, I have moved away from Irvine but I left reassured that Petey would be ok during the travel based on Dr. Kwon's recommendations and prep for the flight. Petey did great and now we are a world away.

Thanks for the wonderful care you provided and best wishes!</Text>

< review>
Dr. Kwon and his staff are absolutely wonderful. I have been bring in my two pups for over a year now and I have any nothing put positive experiences. My dogs are a little shy, but they love seeing Dr. Kwon.

They provide a lot of services from vaccines to surgeries (cats and dogs only). I have also brought in my dogs for ear infections and dental extractions. Each time Dr. Kwon and his staff have been stellar in how they handle my dogs. My dogs are a little nervous around larger dogs and they always try their best to make sure my dogs are comfortable in the back and not stressed in the back when they are away from me.

The office is super nice and always clean! Every time I walk in his friendly staff is always there to greet me and check in on how I am doing as well as how my dogs are doing. Everyone treats us wonderfully and is always trying to be as accommodating as possible. Not only the staff are great, but the doctor is too.

Dr. Kwon is a very compassionate and understanding vet. He makes sure he has the time to thoroughly explain what is going one with my dogs and any procedures that. He draws great diagrams on MS paint so that I see all the different things going on with my dogs. He doesn't make me feel dumb when I ask him for clarification or to explain something again. He also never pressures me into any treatments or procedures I feel uncomfortable with.

I don't know what David was talking about when he said the prices where 3x higher than other pet hospitals in the area. I did some price showing before my first visit and his prices were about the same if not less than the neighboring hospitals.

Overall I would give this hospital a higher score if I could. I have nothing but positive things to say. If you are looking for an affordable and caring vet, give Dr. Kwon and his staff a look. You and your pets won't be disappointed.<//review>

<Gmap_id>0x80dcdeea521b9301:0x368851cb1eb0c88d</Gmap_id><review>Ahmed is a magician with the scissors!

I'm originally from New York and after moving to Irvine in 2018, finding a barber wasn't easy.

The cheap barber for $25 will cut your hair in 5-10 mins. A $40 haircut from supercuts or Danckut's is inconsistent because the barber keeps changing and overall not worth the price.

Ahmed's consistent haircut is high quality for only $35! I usually leave with a good tip because he does such a good job!

What attracted me to his shop was the 100+ positive yelp reviews. What kept me coming back was the confidence boost I get from a haircut from Tesoro.

He knows exactly how to style my hair without needing lots of details. After a while, I just ask for the usual and it comes out perfect every time.

Ahmed is a one man show and for good reason. No one can do a better job than this craftsman!

If you're in the Orange county area you MUST visit this man and see the transformation happen before your eyes!<//review>< Pictures>

I think the owner, who is the barber, is a very personable person. It was a bit too "personable" for me, although it is better than your average retaining tactics, it is a better form.

I appreciate form. Regardless, good nature and friendliness should never substitute expertise, and boundaries, which on those two, there was a subtle lack.

I called for an appointment, I asked for a time and price, I was quote $30.

I had two pictures with me, but the length of the cut was shorter than on the picture, and the style wasn't what it shows.

I then asked him for a specific cut that is at the length it was, it was a familiar cut for me, and I have been to several locations for it. I know how long, and how many tries it should take for it to be done on skill levels. It took several communications to get close to this basic cut. I'm still going to have to go elsewhere to have it cleaned up a bit.

The entire appointment has already taken some time to complete the cut (despite his talking), and that, was brought up to me when I visited the next night to pay him in cash.

This shop doesn't accept credit cards. I hesitate using checks. It was late and so the decision was to pay him in cash the next day.

He gave me back $5 without me mentioning the price difference when I went back, I gave him back the $5 questioning him why.  I didn't see the price list until now.

I was invited to a demonstration of using wax, which I thought was nice of him. It was a brief rinse, semi-dry and the demonstration of wax over gel. There was also offerings of a string scraping thing for a facial hair found on me. Very nice of him, however expertise and professionalism will win over any gesture, that is, for me, every single time, in a business transaction.</review>

Anne Ayunan<//name>
< text>
I have been to almost all Katsu-ya locations -- Hollywood, Glendale, Brentwood, Sherman Oaks, Encino, and Studio City.

The best and most memorable service at a Katsu-ya has been at their Sherman Oaks location on Sepulveda Blvd. I highly recommend visiting this location as their sushi chefs are friendly, prompt, attentive, and their staff including their manager interacts with the guests. He also offers water to those waiting for a seat.

This Katsu-ya location has the worst service out of all the locations I've been visiting over the past 13 years. They are inefficient and disorganized here.

I left Kiwami tonight without finishing our meal because of their horrible level of service. I should have left $0 for tip.

We left  and visited the neighboring original Katsu-ya Studio City location (and paid for valet again at their neighboring sister restaurant) to finish off our meal including dessert.

I vowed to never return to Katsu-ya if we received the same level of service at the original location.

Reasons for our dissatisfaction at Kiwami (upscale Katsu-ya):

-Gave my sister a pot of hot water instead of tea. I've never seen that before.

-The server called me "sir" when I am a female

-Sushi chef forgot our sushi orders

-The wait for sushi sitting at sushi bar was the longest ever I have ever experienced.  I found our sushi chef was too busy to take care or remember our orders.

-They forgot our edamame

I'd stick to the original Katsu-ya locations in Studio City and Encino. Why pay $1 - $4 or so more for a better atmosphere and lack of service?< /text>
